MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Petrona-Regular', Everything looks good.

Petrona Italic (Petrona-Italic[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Petrona-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

'PetronaItalic-SemiBold'
It won't break functionality, but is useless.

Underline Position and Thickness

Underline Position and Thickness

Pass

Petrona Regular (Petrona[wght].ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-110'.
underlineThicknes is '60'.

Pass

Petrona Italic (Petrona-Italic[wght].ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.
